SPEC POSTCONDITION (checked as ASSERT in CTC)
------------------------------------------------------------------------
  _result in dom(Rev')

------------------------------------------------------------------------
DETECTION ANALYSIS
------------------------------------------------------------------------
  Full delivery flow: order progressed to 'delivered' status (owner ×3 + agent ×1 updates). With B7, POST /api/reviews returns 400 for delivered orders (inverted guard). Factory checks resp.statusCode==201; returns Num(400). Spec asserts _result in dom(Rev'). 400 is not a reviewId → ASSERTION FAILS.

  Key failing assertion:
    in(_result17, dom(tmp_Rev_1)) → false [POST /api/reviews returned 400 — delivered order rejected by inverted guard]
